Hello,

I've put the HTML (generated from MD) and PDF versions of the World 
Factbook generated from the JSON output of the Factbook gem online:
http://messetool.vdma.org/messetool/cal/view_static/index.md

When visiting the site with Chrome or Chromium you will see a language 
selector -- Google translate applied to the World Factbook --> more than 
80 computer generated translations online :-) I have no idea why Google 
translation doesn't work with FF and IE (at least for me)....

As promised, attached some collected data and translations as announced 
earlier this week. Dedicated to the public domain.

Cheers
